         <div class="section cmp_richtext">
          <div class="richtext_wrapper ">
           <p>We put the best flight and hotel packages together for you so you don’t need to search for your flight and hotel separately. Just enter the dates of when you want to get away and we will do the rest! Our packages offer savings on the total price of your flight and hotel. There’s plenty to choose from, including destinations in Europe to those further afield, such as New York and Las Vegas. However long you want to go for, lastminute.com has great weekend and short break deals.<br><br></p>
           <h2>New York</h2>
           <p>Head to New York and you’ll land in one of the world’s greatest cities. This is the ideal destination if you’re looking for culture and big-city excitement, with so much to do that you’ll want to come back again and again. You’ll want to see all the big hitters – stand and marvel at the Statue of Liberty, reach the top of the Empire State Building, and visit the electric wonderland that is Times Square. You’ll want to treat your taste buds to mouthwatering lasagne in Little Italy, and delicious Dim Sum in Chinatown. If you’re into art you’ll want to head to the Museum of Modern Art, the Metropolitan Museum of Art, and the Guggenheim Museum. Sports fans will want to see baseball at the Yankee Stadium or basketball at Madison Square Garden. From the Brooklyn Bridge to the Rockefeller Centre, New York is full of places to visit.<br>&nbsp;</p>
           <h2>Las Vegas</h2>
           <p>An oasis of lights in the middle of the Mojave Desert, Las Vegas is the party capital of the world. If you decide to head here you can expect 24-hour casinos, extravagant hotels and countless live shows. Travel down the Las Vegas Strip and there’s the Hollywood-themed MGM Grand, the surreal wonderland of Circus Circus, the Egyptian Luxor and the towering Stratosphere. Enter any of these casinos and it can feel like you’ve been transported to another world, complete with themed bars, and an unbeatable line-up of world-class acts performing each night. Away from the casino floor there’s criminal history in the Mob Museum, thrilling rides in the Adventuredome, and the iconic Graceland Wedding Chapel. From the grand Bellagio to the famous Hard Rock, Las Vegas is a city like no other.<br>&nbsp;</p>
           <h2>Dubai</h2>
           <p>World-famous for its luxury shops, spectacular architecture and vibrant nightlife, Dubai is an unforgettable destination and a great choice for a city break. Towering over the redeveloped city is the ground-breaking Burj Khalifa, the world’s tallest building. Breathtaking panoramas can be enjoyed from one of two observation decks, as well as from the 122<sup>nd</sup>&nbsp;floor restaurant. Shoppers will fall in love with the luxury outlets in the vast Dubai Mall. Of course, no visit to Dubai is complete without spending some time on the white sands of Jumeirah Beach, but when the heat gets too much you can always cool down at the Wild Wadi Water Park. After you’ve stocked up on designer clothes in the mall you can learn about the history of the city at the Dubai Museum, or marvel at the traditional architecture of the Jumeirah Mosque. After a day of shopping and sightseeing, make your way to one of Dubai’s many bars and clubs to dance the night away. A city break in Dubai sticks in the mind long after you’ve left it.&nbsp;</p>
           <p>&nbsp;</p>
           <p>Booking a flight and hotel with lastminute.com means you will always get the best late deals. We pride ourselves on our deals and that’s why lastminute.com gives you a Price Match Guarantee. If you find flight and hotel deals cheaper anywhere else within 24 hours, we will refund the difference. Moreover, the flights and hotels packages offered on lastminute.com are guaranteed under the ATOL scheme, meaning your package is protected if your tour operator or flight carrier becomes insolvent.</p>
          </div>
